{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{a00491_aa36dd4c5217eefc60b6fbf639003b1c6}{Track\+Timebase}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Timebase of Pro Tools track. 

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DynamicPropertyType}{DynamicPropertyType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{a00491_ae22ce161e9b332b856e17f34e017c70f}{Dynamic\+Property\+Type}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Available types of dynamic properties. 

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
